O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	O you, dear children of mine, I have completed this book which is the final word on the science of medicine as a whole, and I have finished it with its explanations and declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And it came to me in a vision that I should complete this treatise with this book, which is part of the work of hands, that is to say "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is dealt with in our region and is strange to all and every part, it is very rare in science and practice, and is not delayed by the little descriptions in books of the ancient ones that the hands have moved.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And from this has come error and vanity, and intentions are closed and science is distant.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	I believe this to be alive with the order of this practitioner according to the path of exposure and statement and acceleration.
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	and I will come with the forms of the tools of cauterization, and of other instruments of the work, with the aid of the statement and preparation of him, as is fitting.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And for the reason that no good master of hands is found in our times, the art of medicine is diminished.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And he who meddles in this should overcome in the science of anatomy, as Galen says, as far as he knows the judgment of members, and their shapes and connections and separations of bones, and has knowledge of bones and nerves and veins and the number of joints, and the movement and moving veins and the resting and non-resting places, and the place of their issue.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	And for this do I say that it is not good with the non-moist, and with work is little;
et meismement en l’art de main.	and more often in the art of hands.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	We tell you in the introduction of this book that who is not knowledgeable about the things before mentioned should take care not to make a mistake and harm men.
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	since I have often seen many of those who meddle in this science and abandon themselves to it without experience.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	For I saw a foolish man who pricked an abscess on the scrofula of a woman or on the neck;
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	So many deaths occurred that women died between his hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	And I saw another wonder, a stone carried by an elderly man; the stone was large;
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	he took with him a piece of the bladder, and died honorable man within three days.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	And I have seen some who were called in to treat the patient and saw the condition of the disease and the size of the stone; and if they treated him, he would surely die.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	And I saw another wonder, a duke of our land who had his leg broken, and with the break there was a wound;
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	and the mirages of ignorance restrained the break over the wound as if by strong ligature, and left no scar on the wound, and left it thus; and so I finished;
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	and he commanded that he should not remove it;
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	and he waited until the leg was completely healed and the wound closed, and came to perdition.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	I was called upon to go to him, and I hurried to remove the leg;
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	and when I dislocated it, he was at peace and felt no pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	But all the ways of corruption were already confirmed in that member, and it cannot be healed;
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	and the corruption did not cease to spread through the member as long as the members were completely lost.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And I saw another wonder that will destroy the abscess and putrefaction, and then inflame because of the evil of its lordship.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For leprosy, when it is infected with melancholy humor, does not come to an end except that one touches it with iron if it is in a suitable place so that one can completely remove what is corrupted.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	And for this, fine children, you must know that the work of hands is divided into two divisions:
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	that is to say, work in which there is danger in many dispositions;
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	and I will show in each of the books of this book where there is fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	For you must keep it so that the wrong man cannot speak ill of you.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	Take your weapons in agreement, undertake your ailments lightly and firmly, and use the best way so that, by the grace of God, you come to salvation and are freed;
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	and leave the expectorable diseases of pain health.
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	and keep your arms away from that which makes you doubt, and have faith that you can come from this world to the other of glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	Galien adds in some of his admonitions:
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	Do not take on the care of a sick person unless you are called a fool.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have devised this treatise according to III chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	The first chapters are fire cauterizations and medicinal water cauterizations, and the chapters ordered of meat just until the feet;
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	and forms of instruments, and iron tools for cauterization, and all that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	The second chapters are about cutting and drilling, and suction cups and wounds, and extractions of arrows, and similar things;
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	and the chapters ordered and forms of instruments.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	The third chapter is about restoring dislocations and torsions and similar things.
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	and it is ordered that the heads of the bones be cut off, and the forms of the instruments be formed.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	Thus, let us remember the work; it is necessary that I give you the quality of aid and the harm of each complexion.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	I say that the qualities of help, and harm, are the most distant words and subtle knowledge and secret responses have been said.
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	and of these many wise men spoke, and agreed upon this.
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	And I am satisfied with few words, for I shorten the length.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	I say that cauterization helps all complexions or it has matter, except for one complexion:
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	that is to say complexion with heat and matter, and complexion with dry and matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	In a hot and dry complexion together with matter, they devised nothing and said that cauterization is great help;
et li autre dirent le contraire:	and the other said the opposite:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	what fire cautery is good for disease that comes from heat and thirst.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	For the natural power of fire, if it is hot, and should not be used to treat a hot disease by heat, nor by thirst;
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	and says that what opposes it does great help for a hot and dry disease that comes from within men.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	For when you compare the body of man with the fire's moisture to the skin, you find the body cold.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree with this word.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have never found it by experience.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	And all roads, don't meddle with fire except he who has experienced it and knows by long practice the chaplet of cauterizing, and the diversity of complexions of men, their dispositions and causes of their diseases, and the remedies and space of time.
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	of other complexions we have no fear, nonetheless with cold and moist diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And all the hair should come together and agree with the fire cautery.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	And know, children, that fire cautery together if there are secrets of healing, and much greater goodness than medical fire cautery.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For fire is simple, and comes only to the member that is cooked, and does not hurt any other member at all.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	The burning remedies come from one member to another by removing, and bring to the member great relief of disease;
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	and perhaps awaken the disease.
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	Fire, because of its height and the goodness of its substance, does not produce this unless there is an excess.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	And I have found this by experience and through the length of service and study that I have put into the art, and it is based on the truth of things;
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	and I apologize for the length of the speech, for it does not please me that you should learn the secret of fire from another, and the quality of the work, how it dispels the diseases of the body, as the philosopher says in demonstrating;
or le recevez en vos pensees.	or receive it in your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	And know, son, that they should be made in what time they should be performed, and they should be prayed.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	And I say that cauterization is suitable at all times, because the harm that overtakes is due to the aid of cauterization;
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	and most often cauterization is done for necessary and urgent pains that cannot be put up with until the time when greater evil comes to the limb.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	And I do not think ever, dear son, as they do so foolishly.
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	For the disease that is cured by cauterization has no return.
et il le dient ensi;	and he should serve in this way;
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	but he does not know how to cauterize, for a cautery is only medicine that moves the complexion and dries up the humors that cause pain; and it is superior to medicine in terms of its swiftness, and because of its virtue and majesty.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	And they can achieve what the disease will do according to the complexion of the patient and the location of the disease and its virtue;
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	and they are gathered together in it the excesses by the acquisition of meat and similar things, unless cauterization is administered at the place where he has lost some excess and moisture, so that cauterization by the heat, and the similar things, and the pain does not return.
mais ce avient poc.	but this did not happen.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	And many people do not understand why the last remedies of medicine are called, and it is seen;
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	but they do not believe that the last remedies of medicine are worth anything, but their intentions are false, and this is a remedy of medicine because when we administer ways to cure in any disease and they don't work, then let us administer this remedy, and it works.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	And so open well that the fire cautery is a medicine derived from the entrails, not according to the intention of foolish lookers.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	The ancient ones said that the gold instrument is more effective than the iron one, and they only mentioned the quality of gold and its high substance;
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	and they said that the fire of the cautery does not cause blisters, but this is not true because I have tested it, and I found that it is true in some people;
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	and a gold cautery works better than an iron one, as they used to say.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	And anyway when you heat the instrument of gold, you are not yet when it is warmed by the color of gold, and soon cools down again;
et s’on le chaufe trop;	and if it is overheated;
si font au feu;	if heated in the fire;
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	then there is sufficient obstruction.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And for this reason we use the fire cautery that we have made ready for our work.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or vos ai ordeneit cet chapitre des lou chief jus'à piez, pour ceu que li voie soit plus legiere à trover.
dou cautere olivaire	The olive oil cautery:
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	The olive oil cautery is useful for a moist and cold forehead, and also for a multitude of problems in the hair, and in the ears, and for many kinds of headaches and pain in the jaw and throat, and especially for all manner of diseases that come from coldness, such as paralysis, swelling, apoplexia, and similar illnesses.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	The form of this cautery is that the patient should be purged by a soluable medicine which clears the head (III or IV), according to what the virtue and ease and the custom of the disease allow him to bear;
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	and then make ready the head of the patient.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	And then make it sit crosswise between your hands, and place his hands on his chest;
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	Afterwards, put the root of your palm on the root of his nose between his two eyes;
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	and let your two hands come together, so that it bleeds from the bridge then heat the cautery which is called "oliver", of which this form is:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	And place your hand slowly and carefully, little by little, while moving it.
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	then release your hand slowly, and feel the joint until you feel the bone just a little.
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	and if you don't feel it, start the fire again as I told you, until you feel the bone.
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	after, take a piece of string, put some cotton on it, and place it over the joint, and leave it for three days;
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	after, put some damp cotton on it.
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	and leave it on until the bone starts to hurt;
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	after, treat the wound with a poultice called "tetrarch", until it heals.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	And they say that as long as the wound is left open, it will heal faster.
et por ce si aide mues.	and so if they help.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And said the ancient that the longer a wound remains open, the more it will putrefy; and therefore if the fire should burn so much of the bone as to be consumed, then remove what is burned from the bone, and let it be cured.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	And so the other one that should be cauterized should be done with care on, and press so strongly it moves the bone as far away as I can put in a woman's vagina to get the humors out.
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	and so the wound must remain open for a long time.
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	after, one must cure and take care of it.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	And these two ways of cauterizing do not seem good to me in all cases, except in some men where there is doubt.
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	and it seems to me that I should let him be.
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	for the shoulder is weakened by continuous solutions of nature, as we witnesses in other limbs;
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	and even if the shoulder of the sick person is weak by nature, and the first impression of cauterizing is more saved and softened for me, and I use it in such a way that it can be cured;
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	of the old woman's pain with her head
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	When in all the head comes chronic pain, and lasts a long time, then the patient must use herbs and pills which are called "cochineals", and head purgation and oils and poultices.
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	and if one does the cautery that we have spoken of above, and it is not useful.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	Take care that the head of the patient is of strong nature, and that he is not too cold;
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	then cauterize him with fire a little as we have spoken above.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	After, make the fire cautery on each horn of the head up to the bone, as we have said before, and make the fire cautery where it is called "vessels";
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	and put them in places where ventouses are placed;
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	and adjust your hand so that you do not see the bone at all:
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	The patient feels an even greater amount of pain with this treatment than with others, and I will speak of it later on.
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	And it is necessary that the corns be cut more finely than those from which one cuts the hair of the head, and this is the form:
dou cautere dou chief	To cauterize the head.
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	When sudden pain comes to a part of the head and extends all the way to the oil, and the shoulder is clean with medicinal oil, and all other treatments I mentioned in the section on diseases have been performed, then there is no benefit.
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	Then it is treated according to two methods, namely with medicinal oil and fire.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	The medicinal oil treatment is done by prying open a tooth with a lever and then cutting off the bark and peeling it down to the bone in two pieces, and then applying it to the head where the pain is in one part, so that you can remove the bark from the leather.
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	and when it is set back if the strapping and restraint are good and left so for XII hours;
et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III;	then unbind it and treat with oil of garlic, and leave the wound for II or III days;
puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	then put on cotton dipped in butter as long as it can be made to adhere;
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the treatment with ointment as long as he is healed;
et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	and if you see that any of the medicinal preparations I have written about or one of the treatments for burning medicines are effective;
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	The fire cautery if it is according to this manner.
Chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Heat the fire cautery so that it is hot:
Et est apelez «clos» por ceu que li chief est fait a la forme d’un clo ou il ait I poc de corbeure, et em mileu a une petite apparance;	And it is called "clos" because the head is made in the shape of a cloak or has a little curl, and is shaped in the middle to a small appearance;
et le met sor le leu dolorous, et tien ta main et trestorne le feir un poc legierement, tant que li moitiez de l’espés dou keur soit arse;	and place it on the painful spot, and hold your hand and turn the fire a little bit, so that half of the heat of the cure is burned;
et lieve ta main que li artere n’arde, que est defuers, et decorre habundance de sanc.	and place your hand so that the artery does not burn, which is far away, and abundant blood flows.
Aprés met coton en awe de seil, et met sor le leu par III jors;	After putting cotton in a string, and placing it on the area for three days;
puis i met coton moilliet em burre, et puis cure le leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	then put cotton wet with oil on it, and then treat the area with ointment until it is healed;
et se tu vuelz cauterize ceste emigraine avec le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare», a tout la pointe, et te garde de coper l’artere en ceste emigraine qui n’est mie anciaine.	and if you want to cauterize this headache with the cautery that is called "cultellare", do so at the tip, and be careful not to cover the artery in this headache that is not old.
de emigraine	of headache
Quant tu cures emigraine si com nos avons devant dit en divisions des maladies, et ne profite mie, et vois que li cauteres devant dis de la medicine et dou fer ne li soffit mie, adonques covient il que tu eschaufes le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare» tant qu’il soit blans;	When you treat the headache as we have said before in the divisions of diseases, and do not benefit from it, and see that the cautery in front of the medicine and the fire does not suit it, then you must heat the cautery that is called "cultellare" until it is white;
et seigne ainsois sor le leu doillant une ligne de demi doi de lonc, et oste ta main une fois, et l’estrain que tu ne coper l’artere et que ne viegnes jusc’a l’os;	and so thus on the limb aching a line of half a foot long, and hold your hand once, and strain that you do not cover the artery and that you do not come to the bone;
et te warde de la mandibule que muet quant on menjut, et li ners n’ait regart que la muet et que spasmus ne veigne a malaide, et te warde de decorrement de sanc de l’artere quant elle sera copee, ou copement ait grant paour et meismement a celui que ne s’i conoit, et qui n’est estudians et esprovez;	and beware of the jaw which moves when it is pulled, and the joint does not rest but shakes and spasm comes to the disease, and beware of the separation of blood from the artery when it is cut, or separation has great fear and more for those who do not know it, and who are not students and tested;
et laisse l’uevre em mi voie;	and leave the work in mid-air;
mais je vos dirai coment on restainche sanc quant li artere est copee, et je vos mostrerai a leu ou il afiert en cest livre.	but I will tell you how to strain blood when the artery is cut, and I will show you at this place in this book.
Et se tu vois que cist cauteres ne soffise mie a la maladie, et li malaides est soffrans, cauterize le enmi le chief ausi com nos avons dit, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And if you see that this fire cautery does not suffice to the disease, and the patient is suffering, cauterize him in mid-air as well as we have said, and heal the wound until it is healed;
et se tu vues, aministre le cautere que nos avons dit ou chapistre de l’estraction de l’artere, avec le cautere qui ait II coutelz;	and if you see, administer the cautery that we have said or chapitre of extraction of the artery, with the cautery that has II knives;
et est cist cauteres millors de celui et plus aidans.	and this cautery is better than that and more helping.
de la dolor des oreilles de part froidor	for pain in the ears from cold
Quant en l’oreille vient dolor de froit, et on i a ovreit de medicines solutives et des autres cures que nos avons dit en la division, et li dolors ne se muet, adonques eschaufe cest cautere qui est apelez «poins», de coi ci est li forme:	When there is pain in the ears from cold, and one has applied the liquid medicines and other treatments we spoke of in the division, and the pain does not go away, then heat this poultice that is called "poins," which has this form:
Aprés pointoie tout entor l’oreille malaide, ou entor les II se la dolor tient en ambedous, et t’esloigne un poc ensus de la racine de l’oreille puis que tu as signiet le leu d’enche;	After puncturing all around the ear on the sore side, or around the two sides where it hurts most, and moving away a little from the root of the ear then that you have found the place of the ache;
et ait X poins entor chescune oreille;	and there are X points inside each ear;
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After healing the place as long as it is healthy.
de la torture de la bouche	of the torture of the mouth
Torture qui doit estre curee par cautere nen est fuers que de celles que muevent de fleume, si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladie;	The torture that must be cured by cautery is only effective for those that move with fluid, as we have said in the division of illnesses;
et ne faire point de cautere as semblances que vienent de sechor et de spame de ners.	and not to use cauterization for similar things that come from scorching and spam of nails.

l’une en la racine de l’oreille, et l’autre un poc defuers la temple, et le tier en l’ajostement des II levres;	one at the root of the ear, and another a little way back from the temple, and the third in the joining of the two lips.
et met le cautere en la partie qui apert saine, et li fai cautere endroit le chief de l’oreille desus un poc desoz la corne dou chief, et un autre en la temple ausi longe com uns poce;	and place the fire cautery in the healthy part, and make a fire cautery at the top of the ear near the corner of the head, and another in the temple as far back as one small finger.
et laisse le cautere tant sus que li moitiez dou keur soit arse;	and leave the fire cautery there until half of the cur is burned away.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	This is how the fire cautery should be made:
Et est li semblance dou cutellaire que nos avons mise devant, mais il est un poc plus subtilz et covient que li coutelz soit un poc plus gros;	And it is the shape of the scalpel that we have described before, but it should be slightly thinner and the blade slightly thicker.
aprés cure lou leu si com j’ai devant dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After fire cauterizing as I have described above, until he is healthy again.
Quant apoplexie est ancieinne et tu la cures ensi com nos avons dit, et il ne profite mie, et li malaides n’ait fievre, adonques li fai IIII cauteres:	When the apoplexy is old and you treat it as we have described above, and it does not improve, and the patient has no fever, then make four fire cauter
II sus les II cornes dou chief, et I emmi le chief, et I ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz» si com nos avons devant dit, et lou derrien cautere sus la bouche de l’estomac;	II under the two horns of the head, and I cut off the head, and I put on the vastez as we have said before, and cautery to the mouth of the stomach.
et soit curez si com nos avons dit devant.	and be cured as we have said before.
de litargie	of chalk

de la froidor dou chief	of the cold
Il covient que li chief soit mundifiez de yeres et de ceu que nos avons devant dit;	It is necessary that the head be cleansed of years and of what we have said before;

de l’epilempsie	of epilepsy
Li epilentiques ne doit useir de cautere fuers que cil qui est fleumatique, et covient premier mondifier le cerveil de yeres et d’autres cures que nos avons dites en la division quant li malaides est grans et soffrans de penre medicine.	of the epileptic should only use fire cauterization if it is phlegmatic; first, the brain should be cleaned of years and other cures that we have mentioned in the division when the patient is great and suffering from pain.
Et se c’est uns enfes qui ne lou puisse soffrir, se li fai gargarisme et mastication mondifiant le cerveil sovent avec bones viandes;	And if it is a child who cannot tolerate the poultice, let him gargle and chew the head with boned meat often;
aprés li reis lou chief em mileu, et i fai I cautere selonc ce que nos avons dit devant, et I cautere sus lou vassel, et sus chescune corne;	after the king has eaten rice in the middle, and I apply the poultice according to what we have said above, and I apply the poultice on the vessel, and on each horn;

Quant par la cause de melancolie sunt les superfluitez ou les moistors corrumpues et fleume grosse, adonques lou cauterize de teils cauteres com nos avons dit a celui qui ait paralisie. aprés presente le linement, et vaut mues de burre de berbis ancien;	after presenting the linen, and dry with old butter;
et lou chaufe a feu tempreement, si que li dois s’on li boute le puisse soffrir;	and heat it moderately over fire, so that the two may drink of it without suffering;
aprés vuide le cercle par dedens emmi le chief, et lou laisse refroidier;	after vacuuming the circle from within by drawing up the head, and allowing it to cool;
et fai ce a malaide chescune semaine une fois avec autre governement boin, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and do this for the sick person every week with good governance, until he is well again.
Ou se tu vues cauterize lou en faisant poins plusors a tot le cautere.	If you want to cauterize yourself by making many punctures all over the cauterization.
Ceste maniere de cautere amoistit le cerveil igaument;	This way of cauterizing wetttens the skull slightly;
et puis met sus coton moilliet en burre et en graisse de geline.	and then put on cotton wet with butter and linseed oil.
de l’awe des eulz	of the eyes
Quant awe vient premierement as eulz par les signes que j’ai dit en la division, adonques encomence et done boivre au malaide chose mundifiant le chief, et le warde de toutes moistors, et lou fai suer ou bain plusors fois a jeun.	When the hair comes first as long by the signs that I said in the division, then begin and do drink to the patient purifying thing the head, and the ward of all moisture, and let it sweat or bathe many times on an empty stomach.

et cope a tout le cautere toutes les voines et les arteres que sont desoz le keur, et soient li cautere lonc selon lou large de la temple;	and wrap all the fire cautery around all the veins and arteries that are exposed, and let the cautery be long according to the width of the temple;

et aucune fois fait on cautere ou hatereil desoz les II os derrier.	and never does one make a fire cautery or hurt while exposing the two bones behind.
dou cors des larmes	The tears of the heart
Quant les larmes des eulz sont ancienes et acostumees et sont sus les voines, ou delez les arteres que sont en l’aparance dou chief defors;	When the tears of the eyes are old and accustomed and are on the veins, or choose the arteries that are in the appearance of the head from behind;

et s’il i a besoigne plus, si le cauterize saigement desus le sorcil a tout I petit cautere.	And if it is needed more, if the cauterize bleeds over the brow to all small cauterize.
dou cors des larmes par dedens les eulz	The tears flow from the heart into the veins.

Quant li papiere de l’oil est mollifie de maladie et de moistor, adonques la cautarize de cest cautere qui est apelez «olivare».	When the paper of oil is softened by disease and moisture, then the cauterization with this cautery which is called "oliva
de coi ci est li forme:	So that you know how to make this form:
Et se tu vues si fai II cauteres sus les II sorcis ausi lons com li sorcilz sont;	And if you see, make two cauterizes over the two brows as long as the brows are;
et n’i lassiez mie la main fors que tant que li tierce partie de la papiere soit arse, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit.	and do not let go of my hand except that as long as the third part of the paper is burned, according to the way I have said.
dou poil qui point l’oil	of the hair that drips oil
Aucune fois avient que li poil des oilz sont convertit au pardedens, et poignent l’oil, et i fait on cauteres selonc II manieres:	Until such time as the hair of the oils is turned into the parched skin, and they grasp the oil, then do I make cauterizations according to two manners:
c’est a savoir de feu, ou de medicine ardant.	that is to say, by fire, or by burning medicine.
Ou cautere de feu comande au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient lons et igals;	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even;
et s’il le poignent a lor nassance, se li estraint les eulz qu’il ne se muevent tant qu’il naissent.	and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.

aprés seigne sus la papiere des eulz une figure que soit ausi com li fuelle dou mirte, et soit li comencemens dou signe delez les poilz;	after signing on the paper of the hairs a figure which is also like the feather of the pine tree, and is the beginning of the sign of the hair;

et li signes de la santeit de l’uevre est que tu voies la papiere retraite, et les poilz levez a la pointure de l’oil;	and the signs of the health of the work are that you see the paper退退, and the hairs rise to the point of the oil;

aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the cure of ointment as long as it is healthy.

Li cauteres de medicine ardant est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient grans et igalz, puis fai de parchemin la forme de la foille de mirte;	The medicine's fire cautery is that you instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even, then make a parchment in the shape of a laurel leaf;
puis pren de savon fransois et de vive chalz, de chescun une .З., et broie ensamble bien;	and take French soap and hot salt, each one of them 1/4 ounce, and grind them together well;
et le fai hastanment, si qu’il ne refroide, puis en espant sus la forme que tu es fait sicom la foille dou mirte, et met sus la papiere des eulz;	and do it carefully so that it doesn't cool down, then in the same manner as you made the shape of the laurel leaf, put the hairs on the parchment;
et se li maladie tient en I oil soulement, si doit on ovrer en I, et se en ambedous ausi;	and if the disease only affects one side, then treat it alone, and also treat the other side;
et met desoz l’oil coton moilliet en abin d’uef;	and dip cotton wicking in oil that's moistened with alcohol;

Quant tu as ceu fait longement, si oste la medicine a ton doit.	As you have done for so long, if the medicine sticks to your tongue.
Et quant li mordication sera passee, si leve le leu d’awe, et rewarde se tu vois la papiere levee ausi com s’ele estoit levee par constraignement de feu ou par incision;	And when the mortification has passed, then raise up the place of aw, and note if you see the paper raised as it was raised by constraint of fire or by incision;
et s’il est ensi, si est bien.	and if it is so, then it is well.
Se ceu non, si remet encor de la medicine sus lou leu ou li medicine n’ait ovreit, tant que tes ovraiges soit igalz, et tes eulz mis a point;	If not, then put back the medicine on the place where it has not worked, as long as your hairs are long and even, and your eyes held fast;

Et se t’est mestier que tu te warde bien a ton ovraige par grant warde qu’il ne chiece point de la medicine as eulz.	And if you must guard your wound well, by great care so that it does not break out with the medicine's hairs.
Et se li papiere devient mole aprés, et li poil poignent en l’oil, si recomence la medicine sus celui leu qui est mollifiez de la papiere proprement, ensi com tu as fait devant;	And if the paper becomes soft after it, and the hairs grip in the oil, then begin again the medicine on that place which is softened by the paper properly, in the same way as you have done before;
aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	after the cure as long as he is healthy;
et c’est li forme de la fuelle dou mirte:	and this is the shape of the funnel of the milky way:
Et saichés que li eul des homes sont divers en grandor et en petitece, et selonc ceu soit tes constraignemens;	And know that the eyes of men are different in size and shape, and according to this they are constrained;
et ne soit mie reponue li droite voie a celui cui est li estude de cest art.	and is not reused straight way to him whose study is this art.
de la cure de fistule par cautere	For the cure of a fistula by cauterization:
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere.	When you treat a fistula as we have said in the division of diseases, and your treatments do not benefit, then it is necessary to apply cauterization according to this method.
Comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain;	Instruct the patient to put his head in your lap;
et teigne li menistres son chief entre tes mains en teil maniere qu’il ne se mueve, ne ne demoinne son chief;	and hold the hair of his head between your hands so that it does not move or fall;
aprés met coton moilliet en abin d’uef ou en jus de persillion sus l’oil;	after wet a cotton ball in wine or juice of cherry on oil;
aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz:	after heat the cautery which is sharp;
et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere;	and place it on the head like a feather of a dove, so that the tip of the cautery is:
se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente;	if you can see, if you point from one head to the other, and if you cannot see, if it is like a tent;
mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	but all the same, he who is the master of the craft must move according to your need.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche;	After pressing, the fistula has been opened and treated, and it is dried up;
et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe;	and if it is closed, so that he works, and treats it furiously;
aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie;	after putting the fire cauldron in place, and holding your hand over the cauldron at the part of the neck above the oil, so that your hand does not go mad;
et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	and put the fire cauldron in the oil grease, and spoil it.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you come to the cauterization just to the bone, it would be good.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors;	If not, then restart the cauldron again once more, and if you need more, let it lie for three days;
aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers;	afterwards I put cotton soaked in oil on it, and the cure of the drying ointment until it is well, and if it is well for forty days, then put the corrosive medicine until the bone is uncovered;
et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	and let him rest according to what he came to his chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And I have a way of cauterizing fistulas, which no one of the ancients mentioned.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu;	Hear a pipe, and seal the hole;
aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	Then put in the edge I have a subtle instrument so that it is the form:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc;	and I make in the quantity of one .Z. of pound;
et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil;	and hold your hand firmly, and do not move the patient so that the pound does not run into its oil;
et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe:	and it is necessary that one put on the oil to the patient wet in a basin of water or in a vat:
li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	the pound so as to close the hole of the fistula, and he is healed by marvelous health.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	And if the fistula is healed by the cauterization that we have spoken of, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	But if not, then it is necessary to give a pound to the nose, and to bring back the fistula to the root of the nose according to what one should do in his own place.
des crevaices en levres	crevasses on lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	The mouth sometimes causes crevices in the lips, which are called "hair," and sometimes in the lips of children.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these crevices as we have said in the divisions, and the cure does not benefit, then a small surgical cauterization is performed according to this form:

aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	After he has cured the head of cerotomy as long as he is healed.
de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess from the throat
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule;	When an abscess forms at the root of the throat or in the palate or at the roots of the teeth after a pustule has rotted and fallen away and becomes a fistula.
et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie:	and you treat it as we have said in the divisions, and it does not benefit:

dou movement des dens	dou movement des dens
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain;	When the teeth are softened by moisture and the gums move, and you cure it with medicine and that does not work, then put the head of the sick in your healthy one;
aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent;	After heat the cautery so that its form will come out later in a certain way so that you put a chain on the teeth;
et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent;	and place the hot cautery inside it carefully, and hold your hand so that the patient feels the heat coming from the root of the teeth;
aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit;	After remove your hand and start again the cautery according to your will;
aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	After fill the patient's mouth with salty water, and leave it for an hour and rinse thoroughly.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	And in this way the tooth that was moving is stabilized, and the gums that were softened are tightened, and the moisture that corrupts is dried up.
de la dolor des dens	of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres:	When the toothache comes from cold, or there is coldness or swelling, and medicines do not work, then it is necessary to perform the cautery according to two ways:
et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	and cautery with butter and fire cautery.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain;	with butter cautery is such that you squeeze butter from a cow, and the tip into a teaspoon of iron or gold.
aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez;	then take cotton and wrap it around the tip of a needle, and squeeze it into butter, and put it on the aching tooth gently and keep it until it has cooled down;
et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	and then often as its virtue comes to the root of the tooth, and if you see if moist wool and cotton in butter freeze, and put it on the aching tooth, and put it on hot iron until the fire comes to the root of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;	The combined fire cautery is such that you squeeze a iron or gold wire, and it is thick so that the fire does not come to the mouth of the patient;
aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez;	then heat the cautery, so that it comes out as follows, and put it on the tooth and keep your hand until the cautery has cooled down;
fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	Make it often, for the pain will be worse the next day or the day after.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer;	And the patient should fill his mouth with good butter before applying the fire cautery, and then swallow it.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	This is the form of the cautery:

des scrophules	of the scrofula

Li forme de la cainne:	The form of the cane:

de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement. et c’est li forme:	This is the form:

dou cautere de pleuresin	For the pleurisy cautery

Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the patient has been infected for a long time, and it is clear that one of the two cures mentioned earlier is needed, then it is necessary to try both at the same time.
de ydropisie	About dropsy.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	 cautery does not work for droves, except in the way called "asclepiades".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you have cured it according to the ways that we have said in the divisions, and your cure is not successful, then it is necessary that you do four cauterizations around the boude, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one behind the back on the spine, and one place on the pis;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauterization be well placed near the cure.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	Afterwards, leave the cauterization uncovered for a long time, and do not leave the cure of the patient uncovered after the cauterization;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and the healing would hurry, and the two intentions would be together with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The shape of the cauterization for the stomach is the key that we have before described;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and its two sides are olive-colored, according to what has been said above.
de l’enfleure des piez	of swelling of the parts
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in the person who is hydropic and are pale yellow in color, it is necessary that you cauterize on the back of the foot between the index and middle fingers;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and hold your hand with the cauldron without turning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, lest the pale yellow be burned, and let the cauterization be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After, make two cauterizations on each leg at the point of the scalpel;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the cauldron be long, one behind the knee in front and the other before, between the leg and the thigh;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauterizations on for a long time without washing, so that the blood comes out;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After the treatment described above, you can then proceed with other treatments which we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the house
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When the solution of the stomach comes from cold and moisture, as long as the virtues retain and digest that are in the stomach and in the intestines are affleurant, and cannot be cured by methods of treatment;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient very suffering and of great virtue, so do I grant cautery on the stomach according to what he has spoken before or cautery of the stomach, with the circulating cautery;
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and four cauteries around the navel with small needle-like cauterization, and two cauteries on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see moisture abundant and the patient suffering, then make fire cautery on the knuckle, and I make cautery on each finger, and II small cauterizes in the stomach to take away the great one, for the cure is profitable when there is good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the hemorrhoids are at the foundation, or one or more, and are old and are large cold and moist corrosion, and are cured as we have said in the divisions, and does not benefit, so do cauterize:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	and III on the spine of the back, that which is all from away is seared little by little in tripling, and I sear the navel two times;
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think that his stomach is cold, and the meat does not cook, and one sees swelling of the face, then the face is seared with cauterization as said before, and another on the liver, and another on the cheek, at all cauterization with needle-like cauterization;
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and leave the fire cautery long ten.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After care, let him rest as long as he is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the charred flesh which is called "thela
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut the skin, if you heat the fire cautery that seems like a razor, and then put it all ablaze on the cut skin;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and I leave so long my hand that the cautery comes to the birth of the vein, from which it does not move away;
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do this once or twice, and if there is blood from the skin, then cauterize it each time as we have said;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the treatment with beneficial oils as long as they are healthy;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large fire cautery on the skin, it will be more effective.
de plaie mal curee	of a wound badly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear to have the wound lanced or opened, which we will tell you in your place, then comes a disease that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is no outlet for the blood, and it has risen and become thick with pus and moisture, then you must try to provide a small passage for it, and be careful that you know how much of the remedy is perfect.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After heating the fire cautery that seems like a razor, and then pour it into the fistula according to the quantity that it has entered, and then restart the cautery as long as those cors are burning and corrupting, once, or twice, or three times, according to the quantity of the bespitting;
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and protect against deep nerve injuries, and great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	it may cause a fistula in the middle of the bladder and intestines, so protect these parts, and never cut through the flesh, and think that it is not permanent;
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after healing the wound as long as it is healthy, and if the members are broken, and the matter has been solid for a long time, then know that the wound is completely healed;
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the matter has not become solid, know that the wound is twofold, and the bone is rotten at the root;
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and in this way as we will say about one of these.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When the cold pain comes with rain and strong wind, and does not respond to a woman's treatment, then you must use the fire cautery on both sides of the rain as we have said before;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we cauterize them with milk, then there will be three cauterizations in a row, and they will be more effective.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak due to cold and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then make cauterization in the lower part behind the bladder, where the hair of the testicles grows, and one on each side, and let each cauterization be as long as a fingernail;
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and I make cauterization behind the back, where there is tickling;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let each cauterization be claw-shaped according to the shape described above.
de la marris	of the urinary tract.
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the marrow is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are withered and their termini are delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, there is great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	So then it is fitting that he has III cauterizes in the loins, as we have said in the cautery of the bladder, and two cauterizes for the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let the cauterize be claved, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the viscous moisture descends into the pelvis of the hip, and for this reason it moves from its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and it is found that the department of the pelvis is wet, so it is fitting that you cauterize the patient on the pelvis with I cautery resembling a circle, and sign before the place in the circle around the pelvis as it turns, so that the pelvis is within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if it be such cauterizes as those with which one cauterizes the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if you do not have this ointment, make three ointments of the great olive, and let these ointments be also perfect as all the curers.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat it until he is healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the hip pain
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When the pain comes in the hip box, and it is from cold and moisture, and the patient is cured of that which we have said in the division, and the cure does not work, and the disease is old:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	Then you must purge the patient of large humors with foul pills, or other bad-looking pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After this make a cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the way of the cautery should be according to two ways:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	that is to say together burning medicines, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery if it is according to many ways, of which one is such:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	You shall cauterize the hunchback's back with three triangular cauters according to this form, and do it with great depth and wide space between each cauterization, having the cauters olive-sized.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	No time is spent cauterizing in the middle on top of the hunchback's hump, for there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see, if you cauterize with a circular cauterizer as we have said before in the dislocation of the hump.
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	However, do it in such a way that the circle contains all the hump, and let all the meat be burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in sciatica, when the pain remains in the hip and does not reach up to the thigh or up to the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes up to the thigh and leg, make two cauterizations there where the patient feels pain, and one above the ankle with three parts; on the left side a little.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cautery of the teeth, and let the thickness of the cure be burned.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two or four points or eight points in the cautery called "points
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if the profession is done, he does it more
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	and if he feels that the pain is in his knee and goes up towards his thigh, you make a dental cautery or circular cautery, and be sure to keep all your cauteries so that you do not leave them on for too long, burning the nerves and large arteries, and causing the patient no more harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I have seen many who have done cauterization on the heel of the foot, and left them so much that the leg was all twisted, and the toes as well, and they were pierced and corrupted all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a solution to the belly from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, do cauterization in one and the other, according to this way.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise men say in the cautery of the hach, how it should be done, make it so thick or less thick as a fingernail, or a little less, and between the fingers and between each finger a space as large as a nail.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let the bars of the harness be over two parts, and let them also be like knots, and there is one hand with iron well made;
et c’est li forme:	This is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And let it be heated until it is all red and hot, and then put it on the box of the sick hip, and turn it around the lower back;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and cauterize once again, and let it rest for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then make an ointment of butter, and leave the open wound long;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the cure of ointment until it is healthy.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasius says that we use little of this cautery because of its fear of his breath, and who uses it little;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and however good this is a cauterizer, who can bear it, and where he afflicts himself.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	For the hot medicine cautery, if you make an instrument between which [the margin] of the hole is, and of rain or iron to a long wall, and in height it has two of us, and between each the quantity of the thickness of a dove;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and are above and below, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After you have put on the box of the hip to the lying patient on his back it is in order, and press your hand very much on the box of the hip;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After you have cut out between the two circles of hot wax that is heated in a pot, and let it rest for an hour, and suffer the patient the heat and the pain of it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it gives a burning taste also as fire does;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the taste has passed away, you take your hand with the instrument and raise the hip of soft wax, and leave it thus for three days, and put on butter as much as that which is black from the scorching is taken away;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let him leave three days to perspire in this way;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the following help after the treatment of onions as long as it is healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain extends only to the thigh or only to the leg, make the instrument that you hold according to what you did in the hip gradually;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the way of hot water, and I have written or treated of the correction of medicines.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and live charcoal, as much of one as of the other, and grind them together and put them in a nine-pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	or there is a small opening where the point of a rasp enters;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place there another pot that can be well plugged with ash, and put on alkali and warm water and soft water, until there are two cups of powder that you have well mixed in your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and leave it thus until it has become very thin with water and ash, then take all of this water, and pour it over alkali and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then if it will be wet and is treated with a medicine's excess and other members' cauterization.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it performs the same work as fire does, and if with other medicines one cauterizes well the wound with a mixture of thistle, myrrh, and salt mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galiens tells us of a remedy in which a noble man was cured of the pain in the hip and sciatic leg, and he drank it, and said that another did not cure him, but he was healed in one soul when this remedy was made, and he bathed himself as it is taught hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And it is said that you squeeze green and dry lead with a little fat, and put it on the wound and leg or thigh where the pain holds, and leave it.
